
Cumulocity IoT Open-Source Repository Overview
==============================================


This Repository generates on a daily basis a table of all open-source repositories for Cumulocity-IoT. It should give a brief overview of all available IoT open-source repositories for Cumulocity IoT including additional content at TechCommunity.

Number of Open-Source Repos: **400**


Table of contents
=================

* [10 Newest Repositories](#10-newest-repositories)
* [Open-Source Repository Overview Table](#open-source-repository-overview-table)
* [Open-Source Repository Detail Lists](#open-source-repository-detail-lists)
	* [All Categories](#all-categories)
	* [Microservices](#microservices)
	* [Widgets](#widgets)
	* [Webapps](#webapps)
	* [Agents](#agents)
	* [Examples](#examples)
	* [Clients](#clients)
	* [Simulators](#simulators)
	* [Documentations](#documentations)
	* [Tutorials](#tutorials)
	* [Extensions](#extensions)
	* [CLIs](#clis)
	* [Others](#others)

### [Cumulocity-IoT/cumulocity-dynamic-mapper](https://github.com/Cumulocity-IoT/cumulocity-dynamic-mapper)

**Owner**: Cumulocity-IoT

### [Cumulocity-IoT/cumulocity-microservice-templates](https://github.com/Cumulocity-IoT/cumulocity-microservice-templates)

**Owner**: Cumulocity-IoT

### [Cumulocity-IoT/cumulocity-lora](https://github.com/Cumulocity-IoT/cumulocity-lora)


**Description**: LoRa framework including implementations for TTN, Chirpstack, Kerlink Wanesy, Loriot, Actility, Objenious, Live Objects, Orbiwan as well as many codecs and still adding more, and lot of unique features such as user-friendly UI to send device commands, gateway management, codec IDE

**Owner**: Cumulocity-IoT

**Description**: This is an example for sniffing data packages inside a network and filtering connection packages. ### [qvest-digital/KNIME-Cumulocity-Connector](https://github.com/qvest-digital/KNIME-Cumulocity-Connector)


**Description**: The “Cumulocity Nodes” collection of nodes provides functionality to retrieve information about IoT devices, corresponding measurements, alarms and events from a given Cumulocity IoT platform instance. ### [Cumulocity-IoT/cockpit](https://github.com/Cumulocity-IoT/cockpit)


**Description**: A repository containing the latest sources of the Cumulocity Web SDK based "cockpit" application. It also allows to compare the differences between Web SDK versions for this application easily. To quickly get started using the Web SDK, this application can also be just forked instead of the usualy scaffolding approach.

**Owner**: Cumulocity-IoT

[![Generic badge](https://img.shields.io/badge/category-Other-blue.svg)]() 

[![Generic badge](https://img.shields.io/badge/relation-Cumulocity%20Org-blue.svg)]()
